<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:костить.html>костя́щий</a> (14695)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:костить.html>костя́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kostjáščij</span>)
</p>

***косяк.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:косяк.html>кося́к</a> (6960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:косяк.html>кося́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kosják</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:косяк.html>косяка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:косяк.html>косяки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:косяк.html>косяко́в</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">косячо́к</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shoal, school (a group of fish)</li>
<li>flock (a group of birds)</li>
<li>herd (a group of horses)</li>
<li>jamb, cant, cheek, door-post</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> joint, a marijuana cigarette</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fault, mistake</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:сяк.html>ся́к</a></b>

***кот.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>кот</a> (1300)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kotъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>кот</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kot</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>кота́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>коты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>кото́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кошка.html>ко́шка</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tomcat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>кот</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сапог.html>сапога́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kot</b> v sapogáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Puss in Boots</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>кот</a></b> наплакал</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kot</b> naplakal</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nothing to speak of (next to nothing)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>коту́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:масленица.html>ма́сленица</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>придёт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:великий.html>вели́кий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пост.html>пост</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne vsjó <b>kotú</b> máslenica, pridjót i velíkij post.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">All good things must come to an end; You have to take the rough with the smooth.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купить.html>купи́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>кота́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мешок.html>мешке́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kupítʹ <b>kotá</b> v mešké</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to buy a pig in a poke</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кот.html>кот</a></b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">коти́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kotírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">finance<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to circulate on an exchange, to be listed</li>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">côtelette</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:котлета.html>котле́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kotléta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:котлета.html>котле́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:котлета.html>котле́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:котлета.html>котле́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>meat patty, meatball, frikadelle</li>

***который.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рый</a> (31)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kotorъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷóteros</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kotóryj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>interrogative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> which?
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рую</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хоти́те</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kotóruju</b> knígu vy xotíte?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Which book do you want?</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kotóryj</b> čas?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What time is it?</span></div></li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative pronoun</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> which, that, who
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хочу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежи́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>столе́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja xočú knígu, <b>kotóraja</b> ležít na stolé.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I want the book that is on the table.</span></div></li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The instrumental <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рою</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kotóroju</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is significantly less common than its shortened form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рой</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kotóroj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and overuse of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рою</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kotóroju</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is likely to be felt archaic or dated.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>рый</b>
</p><p>Местоимение, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопросительный.html>вопроси́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:союз.html>сою́з</a>, адъективное <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — lt;1agt;.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-котор-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:коттедж.html>котте́дж</a> (8893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cottage</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коттедж.html>котте́дж</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kottɛ́dž</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коттедж.html>котте́джа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коттедж.html>котте́джи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коттедж.html>котте́джей</a></b>)

***кофе.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a> (1589)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1653. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">قَهْوَة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qahwa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">coffee, a brew, wine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kófe</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>coffee <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in the form of a beverage</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čórnyj <b>kófe</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">black <b>coffee</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молоко́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kófe</b> s molokóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">milk <b>coffee</b> / white <b>coffee</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крепкий.html>кре́пкий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krépkij <b>kófe</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">strong <b>coffee</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чашка.html>ча́шка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čáška <b>kófe</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">a cup <b>of coffee</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>coffee <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in the form of beans</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зерно.html>зёрнах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kófe</b> v zjórnax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">whole-bean coffee</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молоть.html>мо́лотый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mólotyj <b>kófe</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">ground coffee</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растворимый.html>раствори́мый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rastvorímyj <b>kófe</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">instant coffee</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кофеин.html>кофеи́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kófe</b> bez kofeína</i> ― <span class="e-translation">decaf</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The word <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a></b></span> is masculine, but is often informally treated as neuter: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">“горя́чее <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a></b>”</span>. Such usage is usually frowned upon by educated people.</li>
<li>Since the lack of declension is inconvenient for some people, the diminutive forms of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a></b></span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кофеек.html>кофеёк</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kofejók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or the dated/colloquial form <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ко́фий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kófij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, are sometimes used.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кофейный.html>кофе́йный</a> (12136)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кофе́й-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">koféj-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кофта.html>ко́фта</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kófta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кофта.html>ко́фты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кофта.html>ко́фты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кофта.html>ко́фт</a></b>)

<ol><li>jersey, cardigan <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">garment knitted from wool, worn over the upper body</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кофта.html>ко́фта</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kófta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-очка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-očka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кофточка.html>ко́фточка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kóftočka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кофточка.html>ко́фточки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кофточка.html>ко́фточки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кофточка.html>ко́фточек</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочан.html>коча́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kočán</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочан.html>кочана́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочан.html>кочна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочан.html>кочаны́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочан.html>кочны́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочан.html>кочано́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочан.html>кочно́в</a></b>)

<ol><li>head of cabbage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (human) head, noggin

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кочевать.html>кочева́ть</a> (14348)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kyrgyz_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kyrgyz language">Kyrgyz</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ky">көчүү</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ky-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">köçüü</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kazakh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kazakh language">Kazakh</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="kk">көшу</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="kk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">köşw</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Azerbaijani_language" class="extiw" title="w:Azerbaijani language">Azerbaijani</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="az">köçmək</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lead a nomad's life</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, etc. Contains the suffix <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ева́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***кочегар.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кочегар.html>кочега́р</a> (11319)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочегар.html>кочега́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kočegár</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочегар.html>кочега́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочегар.html>кочега́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочегар.html>кочега́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stoker</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>No feminine form exists, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочегарка.html>кочега́рка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kočegárka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> means "stokehold".
</p>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:коченеть.html>кочене́ть</a> (26847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ко́чень</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kóčenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (variant of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочан.html>коча́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kočán</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коченеть.html>кочене́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kočenétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окоченеть.html>окочене́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закоченеть.html>закочене́ть</a></b>)
</p>

***кочерга.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кочерга.html>кочерга́</a> (17808)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>According to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Max_Vasmer" class="extiw" title="w:Max Vasmer">Vasmer</a>, inherited from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> form, probably with the original sense of “stump, stalk”; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочерга.html>кочерга́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kočerhá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кучу́рга</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kučúrga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">koczarga</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">качарга́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kačarhá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">коко́ра</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kokóra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочан.html>коча́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kočán</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Alternatively (but less likely), perhaps a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">күчәргә</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">küçärgä</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to move</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Altai_language" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Altai language">Southern Altai</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="alt">кӧчӱр</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="alt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">köčür</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to relocate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочерга.html>кочерга́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kočergá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочерга.html>кочерги́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочерга.html>кочерги́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочерга.html>кочерёг</a></i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кочерёжка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>poker <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">metal rod for adjusting burning logs or coals in a fire</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">automotive  slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> steering-wheel lock, club lock</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">automotive  slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stickshift, manual gear lever</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">automotive  slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> column-mounted shifter</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***кочка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кочка.html>ко́чка</a> (10067)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочка.html>ко́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kóčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочка.html>ко́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочка.html>ко́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кочка.html>ко́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hummock, tussock, mound, hillock</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ко́ч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-кочк-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>.
